        <script id="search-result-tpl" type="text/x-template">
         <div class="media">
         <div class="media-left">
             <a href="#">
                 <img class="media-object" src="{%=o.image%}" alt="{%=o.name%}">
             </a>
         </div>
         <div class="media-body">
             <h4 class="media-heading"><a href="{%=o.url%}">{%=o.name%}</a></h4>
             {% if (o.price) { %}
                 <div class="price-info">
                     {% if (o.price.type == 'gross_net')  { %}
                         <span class="price">{%=o.price.brutto%}</span>
                     {% } else if (o.price.type == 'net_gross') { %}
                         <span class="price">{%=o.price.netto%}</span>
                     {% } else if (o.price.type == 'only_net') { %}
                         <span class="price">{%=o.price.netto%}</span>
                     {% } else { %}
                         <span class="price">{%=o.price.brutto%}</span>
                     {% } %}
                 </div>
             {% } %}
         </div>
     </div>
        </script>
        <script type="text/javascript">
         jQuery(function($) {
         $('.search').submit(function() {
             var input = $(this).find('input[name=query]');
 
             if (!input.val()) {
                 input.parent().addClass('has-error');
                 return false;
             } 
 
             input.parent().removeClass('has-error');
             return true;            
         });
 
         var products = new Bloodhound({
             datumTokenizer: Bloodhound.tokenizers.obj.whitespace('name'),
             queryTokenizer: Bloodhound.tokenizers.whitespace,
             remote: {
                 url: '/search/typeahead?query=%QUERY',
                 wildcard: '%QUERY'
             },
             limit: 100
         });
                      
         products.initialize();
 
         var tpl = tmpl($('#search-result-tpl').html());
 
         var typeahead = $('#search-top .search input[type="search"]');
         typeahead.typeahead({
             source: products.ttAdapter(),
             messages: {
                 noresults: "Brak produktów dla wybranych kryteriów"
             }, 
             viewport: { selector: 'body', padding: 0 },   
             template: function(suggestions,search_query) {
                 var content = '';
                 var content_categories = '';
                 var content_products = '';
                 var content_printers = '';
                 var query = search_query;
                 var search_url = '/product/search?query='+query;
                 var search_url2 = '/search/search?showAdvance=1&st_search[and_search]=1&query='+query;
 
                 if(typeof suggestions[0] != 'undefined' && suggestions[0].length){
                 for (var i = 0; i < suggestions[0].length; i++) {
                     content_products += '<li data-url="'+suggestions[0][i].url+'">'+tpl(suggestions[0][i])+'</li>';
                 }
                 }                
                 if(typeof suggestions[1] != 'undefined' && suggestions[1].length){ 
                 for (var i = 0; i < suggestions[1].length; i++) {
                     content_categories += '<li data-url="'+encodeURI(search_url+'&cid='+suggestions[1][i].id)+'"><a href="'+encodeURI(search_url+'&cid='+suggestions[1][i].id)+'">'+suggestions[1][i].name+'</a></li>';
                 }
                 }
                 if(typeof suggestions[2] != 'undefined' && suggestions[2].length){
                 for (var i = 0; i < suggestions[2].length; i++) {
                     content_printers += '<li data-url="'+encodeURI(search_url2+'&si_search[model]='+suggestions[2][i].id+'&si_search[producer]='+suggestions[2][i].producer_id)+'"><a href="'+encodeURI(search_url2+'&si_search[model]='+suggestions[2][i].id+'&si_search[producer]='+suggestions[2][i].producer_id)+'">'+suggestions[2][i].name+'</a></li>';
                 }
                 }                
                 
                 if(content_categories.length && content_products.length) {
                 content_categories = '<ul class="list-unstyled catlist">'+content_categories+'</ul>';
                 content_products = '<ul class="list-unstyled prodlist">'+content_products+'</ul>';
                 
                 if(content_printers.length)
                 content_printers = '<h3>Proponowane drukarki</h3><ul class="list-unstyled printerlist">'+content_printers+'</ul>';
                 
                 content = '<li><div class="typeahead-products"><h3>Proponowane produkty</h3>'+content_products+'</div><div class="typeahead-categories typeahead-printers"><h3>Proponowane kategorie</h3>'+content_categories+content_printers+'</div></li>';
                 
                 }else{
                   if(content_printers.length)
                     content = '<li><div class="typeahead-categories typeahead-printers"><h3>Proponowane drukarki</h3><ul class="list-unstyled printerlist">'+content_printers+'</ul></div></li>';
                   else
                     content = content_products;                                 
                 }
                 
                 
                 return content;
             }
         });
     });
        </script>

         <script type="text/javascript">
          //<![CDATA[
 jQuery(function($) {
     var horizontalCategories = $('.horizontal-categories');
     var headerContainer = $('#header-navbar');
     var buttons = $('#navbar-buttons');
     var categories = horizontalCategories.children(':not(.more)');
     var moreContainer = $('<li style="display: none" class="dropdown more"><a data-toggle="dropdown" data-hover="dropdown" class="dropdown-toggle" href="#"><span class="icon-bar"></span><span class="icon-bar"></span><span class="icon-bar"></span></a><ul class="dropdown-menu"></ul>');
 
 
     moreContainer.children("a").dropdownHover();
 
     horizontalCategories.append(moreContainer); 
 
     horizontalCategories.bind('highlight', function(event, href) {
         var $this = $(this);
         if (href) {
             $this.find('a[href="'+href+'"]').parents("li").addClass("active"); 
             $this.data('href', href);
         } else {
             $this.find('a[href="'+$this.data('href')+'"]').parents("li").addClass("active");
         }      
     }); 
 
     function more() {
 
 
         var current = 0;
         var content = '';
 
         moreContainer.hide();
 
         if ($(window).width() < 992) {
             categories.show(); 
         } else {
             horizontalCategories.css({ visibility: 'hidden', 'height': 0 });  
             
             var widthOffset = moreContainer.width() + buttons.width();
             var width = headerContainer.width(); 
             categories.each(function() {
                 var li = $(this);
                
                 current += li.width();
             
                 if (current >= width) {
                     li.hide();
                     var link = li.children('a');
                     content += '<li><a href="'+link.attr('href')+'" class="category-link">'+link.html()+'</a></li>';
                 } else {
                     li.show();
                 }
                 
             });
 
             if (content) {
                 moreContainer.children('.dropdown-menu').html(content);
                 moreContainer.show();
                 horizontalCategories.trigger('highlight');  
             } 
             
         }
   
         horizontalCategories.css({ visibility: 'visible', 'height': 'auto' });     
     }
 
     horizontalCategories.on("click", '.category-link', function() {
         var link = $(this);
 
         if (link.data('toggle') != 'dropdown' || link.data('toggle') == 'dropdown' && link.parent().hasClass('open')) {
             window.location = $(this).attr('href')+'?horizontal';
             return false;
         }
     }); 
 
     var win = $(window);
 
     var throttle = 250,
         handler = function() {
             curr = ( new Date() ).getTime();
             diff = curr - lastCall;
 
             if ( diff >= throttle ) {
 
                 lastCall = curr;
                 $( window ).trigger( "throttledresize" );
 
             } else {
 
                 if ( heldCall ) {
                     clearTimeout( heldCall );
                 }
 
                 // Promise a held call will still execute
                 heldCall = setTimeout( handler, throttle - diff );
             }
         },
         lastCall = 0,
         heldCall,
         curr,
         diff;
 
     win.resize(handler);
 
     win.on("deviceorientation", handler); 
 
     win.on("throttledresize", more);
 
     $(window).one("webkitTransitionEnd otransitionend oTransitionEnd msTransitionEnd transitionend webkitAnimationEnd oanimationend msAnimationEnd animationend", more);
 
     var img = $('#logo img');
     img.one('load', more);
     if (img.get(0).complete || img.get(0).readyState === 4) {
         more();
     } 
 });
 //]]>
         </script>

          <script id="search-result-tpl" type="text/x-template">
           <div class="media">
         <div class="media-left">
             <a href="#">
                 <img class="media-object" src="{%=o.image%}" alt="{%=o.name%}">
             </a>
         </div>
         <div class="media-body">
             <h4 class="media-heading"><a href="{%=o.url%}">{%=o.name%}</a></h4>
             {% if (o.price) { %}
                 <div class="price-info">
                     {% if (o.price.type == 'gross_net')  { %}
                         <span class="price">{%=o.price.brutto%}</span>
                     {% } else if (o.price.type == 'net_gross') { %}
                         <span class="price">{%=o.price.netto%}</span>
                     {% } else if (o.price.type == 'only_net') { %}
                         <span class="price">{%=o.price.netto%}</span>
                     {% } else { %}
                         <span class="price">{%=o.price.brutto%}</span>
                     {% } %}
                 </div>
             {% } %}
         </div>
     </div>
          </script>
          <script type="text/javascript">
           jQuery(function($) {
         $('.search').submit(function() {
             var input = $(this).find('input[name=query]');
 
             if (!input.val()) {
                 input.parent().addClass('has-error');
                 return false;
             } 
 
             input.parent().removeClass('has-error');
             return true;            
         });
 
         var products = new Bloodhound({
             datumTokenizer: Bloodhound.tokenizers.obj.whitespace('name'),
             queryTokenizer: Bloodhound.tokenizers.whitespace,
             remote: {
                 url: '/search/typeahead?query=%QUERY',
                 wildcard: '%QUERY'
             },
             limit: 100
         });
      
         products.initialize();
 
         var tpl = tmpl($('#search-result-tpl').html());
 
         var typeahead = $('#header-navbar .search input[type=search]');
         typeahead.typeahead({
             source: products.ttAdapter(),
             messages: {
                 noresults: "Brak produktów dla wybranych kryteriów"
             }, 
             viewport: { selector: '#header-navbar', padding: 0 },   
             template: function(suggestions,search_query) {
                 var content = '';
                 var content_categories = '';
                 var content_products = '';
                 var content_printers = '';
                 var query = search_query;
                 
                 var search_url = '/product/search?query='+query;
                 var search_url2 = '/search/search?showAdvance=1&st_search[and_search]=1&query='+query;
             
                 if(typeof suggestions[0] != 'undefined' && suggestions[0].length){
                 for (var i = 0; i < suggestions[0].length; i++) {
                     content_products += '<li data-url="'+suggestions[0][i].url+'">'+tpl(suggestions[0][i])+'</li>';
                 }
                 }                
                 if(typeof suggestions[1] != 'undefined' && suggestions[1].length){ 
                 for (var i = 0; i < suggestions[1].length; i++) {
                     content_categories += '<li data-url="'+encodeURI(search_url+'&cid='+suggestions[1][i].id)+'"><a href="'+encodeURI(search_url+'&cid='+suggestions[1][i].id)+'">'+suggestions[1][i].name+'</a></li>';
                 }
                 }
                 if(typeof suggestions[2] != 'undefined' && suggestions[2].length){
                 for (var i = 0; i < suggestions[2].length; i++) {
                     content_printers += '<li data-url="'+encodeURI(search_url2+'&si_search[model]='+suggestions[2][i].id+'&si_search[producer]='+suggestions[2][i].producer_id)+'"><a href="'+encodeURI(search_url2+'&si_search[model]='+suggestions[2][i].id+'&si_search[producer]='+suggestions[2][i].producer_id)+'">'+suggestions[2][i].name+'</a></li>';
                                           
                 }
                 }                
                 
                 if(content_categories.length && content_products.length) {
                 content_categories = '<ul class="list-unstyled catlist">'+content_categories+'</ul>';
                 content_products = '<ul class="list-unstyled prodlist">'+content_products+'</ul>';
                 
                 if(content_printers.length)
                 content_printers = '<h3>Proponowane drukarki</h3><ul class="list-unstyled printerlist">'+content_printers+'</ul>';
                 
                 content = '<li><div class="typeahead-products"><h3>Proponowane produkty</h3>'+content_products+'</div><div class="typeahead-categories typeahead-printers"><h3>Proponowane kategorie</h3>'+content_categories+content_printers+'</div></li>';
                 
                 }else{
                   if(content_printers.length)
                     content = '<li><div class="typeahead-categories typeahead-printers"><h3>Proponowane drukarki</h3><ul class="list-unstyled printerlist">'+content_printers+'</ul></div></li>';
                   else
                     content = content_products;
                 } 
                 
                 
                 return content;
             }
         });
     });
          </script>
         </div>

    <script type="text/javascript">
     //<![CDATA[
 jQuery(function($) {
    if ($('#nav-settings  > ul > li:empty').length == 2)
    {
       $('#nav-button-settings').hide();
    } 
 
 
 
    function menuFix() {     
    
         var scrolled = $(window).scrollTop();
         
                 
               
         if ($(window).width() > 991) {
         
           $('#header-navbar-outer').removeClass('navbar-fixed-top');
           $('#header-navbar-position').css('min-height', '');
                   
           var menuTop = $('.header-top').offset().top;
                                     
             //var menuTop = $('#header-navbar-position').offset().top + menuHeight;    
             if (scrolled > 0) {
             
                 nscart_pos = ($(window).width() - $('#header').width())/2;   
             
                 //$('#header-navbar-outer').addClass('navbar-fixed-top');
                 $('.header-top').addClass('header-top-fixed');
                 
                 $('#nav-shopping-cart').css("right", nscart_pos);
                 $('#nav-shopping-cart').addClass('fixed-nav-shopping-cart');
                 
                 //$('#header-navbar-position').css('min-height', menuHeight - 1);
             } else {
                $('#nav-shopping-cart').css("right", 0);
                 $('.header-top').removeClass('header-top-fixed');
                 $('#nav-shopping-cart').removeClass('fixed-nav-shopping-cart');
                 //$('#header-navbar-outer').removeClass('navbar-fixed-top');
                 //$('#header-navbar-position').css('min-height', '');
             }
 
         }else {
             $('.header-top').removeClass('header-top-fixed');
             $('#nav-shopping-cart').removeClass('fixed-nav-shopping-cart');
             $('#nav-shopping-cart').css("right", 0);
             
 
             var menuHeight = $('#header-navbar-outer').height();
             var menuTop = $('#header-navbar-position').offset().top;
                     
             //var menuTop = $('#header-navbar-position').offset().top + menuHeight;    
             if (scrolled > menuTop) {               
                 $('#header-navbar-outer').addClass('navbar-fixed-top');  
                 $('#header-navbar-position').css('min-height', menuHeight - 1);
             } else if (scrolled < menuTop) {
                 $('#header-navbar-outer').removeClass('navbar-fixed-top');
                 $('#header-navbar-position').css('min-height', '');
             }
         
         
         }
     }
     
     
 
     $(document).ready(function(){
         menuFix();
     });
     $(window).scroll(function(){
         menuFix();
         $('.typeahead-popover').popover('hide')
         $('.bootstrap-typeahead').blur();
     });
     $(window).resize(function(){
         menuFix();
     });
    
 
 });
 //]]>
    </script>

              <script type="text/javascript">
               //<![CDATA[
 jQuery(function($) {
    $(document).ready(function() {
       
       $("body").on("click", ".basket_add_link", function(event) {
          var quantity_selector = '';
          var url = '';
          var parameters = [];
 
          if (event.type == 'submit') {
             var form = $(this);
 
             url = form.attr('action');
 
             if (!quantity_selector) { 
                quantity_selector = '#' + form.attr('id') + '_quantity';
             } 
          
             parameters = form.serializeArray();
 
          } else if (event.type == 'click') {
             var link = $(this);
 
             if (link.hasClass('basket_disabled')) {
                 event.stopImmediatePropagation();
                 return false;
             }
 
             url = link.attr('href');
 
             if (!quantity_selector) { 
                quantity_selector = '#' + link.attr('id') + '_quantity';
             }           
          }
 
          var quantity = $(quantity_selector); 
 
          if (quantity.length && quantity.val() == 0) {
                quantity.val(quantity.get(0).defaultValue);
          }          
 
          if (quantity.length) {
             parameters.push({ name: "quantity", value: quantity.val() });
          }         
 
          if (window.location.protocol != 'https:') {
             url = url.replace('https://', 'http://'); 
          }
 
          var body = $('body').css({ cursor: 'wait' });
          var div = $('<div></div>');
          div.css({ 'height': body.height(), 'width': body.width(), position: 'absolute', 'z-index': 10000, background: 'transparent', cursor: 'wait' });
          body.prepend(div);
 
          $.post(url, parameters, function(html) {
             var html = $(html);
             $('body').append(html);
             div.remove();
             body.css({ cursor: 'auto' });
          }, 'html');
          event.preventDefault();
          event.stopImmediatePropagation();
       });
    });
 });
 //]]>
              </script>

                Po założeniu nowego tonera do drukarki Xerox może się okazać, że drukarka go nie rozpozna. Czy drukarka lub toner były sprowadzane z zagranicy? To może być przyczyna. Ale... bać się nie ma czego.
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>
        <div class="tinymce_html thumbnail clearfix" id="main_text">
         <!--[mode:tiny]-->
         <h3>
         </h3>
         <h3>
          Sklep internetowy Magusz
         </h3>
         <p>
          W naszym sklepie znajdziesz bogatą ofertę ponad 20 000 artykułów największych renomowanych producentów: Brother, Canon, Epson, HP, Konica-Minolta, Lexmark, OKI, Panasonic, Samsun i wielu innych. Posiadamy największy wybór tonerów oraz
          <strong>
           tuszy do drukarek
          </strong>
          pasujących do wszystkich modeli drukarek dostępnych w Polsce. U nas znajdziesz produkty oryginalne min.:
          <strong>
           tusz do drukarki HP
          </strong>
          ,
          <strong>
           tusz do drukarki Brother
          </strong>
          ,
          <strong>
           tusz do drukarki Canon
          </strong>
          oraz zamienniki, które jakością nie odbiegają od produktów oryginalnych. Polecamy również szeroki wybór
          <strong>
           drukarek laserowych
          </strong>
          oraz
          <strong>
           drukarek wielofunkcyjnych
          </strong>
          . Profesjonalne doradztwo, szybki koszt wysyłki oraz atrakcyjne ceny sprawiły, że współpracuje z nami ponad 50 tys klientów. Zapraszamy do zakupów w sklepie internetowym Magusz, jak również do odwiedzenia sklepu stacjonarnego w Warszawie przy ulicy Powstańców Śląskich 85, lokal U2.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          <strong>
           Dołącz do grona zadowolonych Klientów!
          </strong>
         </p>
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
